# About this item
* 7g Ultralight Hook-On Design For A Perfect Fit: Made with 0.6mm ultra-thin titanium filaments and soft liquid silicone, and weighing only 7g, OpenRock S2 flexibly adapts to different ear shapes, ensuring all-day comfort - even during outdoor activities.
* Enhanced Bass &amp; Powerful Sound: OpenRock uses BassDirect technology to channel low-frequency energy from its 12mm transducer directly into the ear canal, delivering enhanced bass with minimal sound loss. With LDAC codec and Hi-Res certification, it supports high-resolution audio transmission, ensuring rich, detailed and high-quality sound.
* Triple Sweat & Water Resistant Design: Scientifically angled construction optimizes your wearing position, allowing sweat to glide away naturally and reducing contact with sweat. The independent BassDirect chamber protects PCBA components from sweat intrusion, while a water-repellent nano-coating on components improves durability.
* Effortless Photography with Remote Camera Control: Simply press the button on the headset to remotely control the camera when your phone is in photo or video mode, making capturing during outdoor hiking easy and convenient.
* 32 Hours Playtime: OpenRock S2 delivers up to 8 hours of playback on a single charge and up to 32 hours with the charging case. A 5-minute fast charge gives you 1 hour of use.
* AI Noise Cancellation with 4 Microphones: Four high-quality microphones use beamforming technology in array configuration, supporting an AI noise canceling algorithm to effectively eliminate ambient noise. With the windproof structure, even in strong winds, your call remains crystal clear.
* Bluetooth 6.0 & Multipoint Connection: OpenRock S2 is equipped with the latest Bluetooth 6.0 for fast transmission and instant pairing. Supports simultaneous connection to two Bluetooth devices with seamless switching.
[See more product details](#productDetails)

3. #### Come iniziamo?
Siamo un produttore audio professionale con oltre 15 anni di esperienza nella produzione audio. Vogliamo condividere una cosa: il potere della musica.
#### Cosa rende i nostri prodotti unici e di alta qualità?
La passione per il sonicato costituisce la base della nostra cultura. I nostri prodotti hanno una qualità del suono acclamata dalla critica e un design ergonomico unico per la perfetta combinazione di comfort e conduzione audio. Più di 1 milione di vendite sono la testimonianza che abbiamo saldamente piantato la bandiera di OneOdio nel settore audio e HIFI in tutto il mondo.

[**How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void(0))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings, help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

Boba
##### *5.0 out of 5 stars*Love these! Super comfortable to wear, minimal sound leak
Reviewed in Canada on 12 July 2025
Colour Name: Black**Amazon Vine Customer Review of Free Product([What's this?](https://www.amazon.it/-/en/gp/vine/help?ie=UTF8))
I've been looking for good open ear headphone especially for when I'm in the office since I want to be able to still hear what's going on around me. I have tried a couple cheaper alternatives with decent reviews, but found them very uncomfortable to wear on my ears, likely due to the shape of my ears. I'm very glad I decided to give this set a try because I found them EXTREMELY comfortable to wear, unlike others I've tried, and completely meets my needs! It barely feels like I'm wearing anything with these on and they don't press on the back of my ears at all. Note I do wear glasses most days and while my glasses make these a bit harder to put on securely, the headphones are still very comfortable to wear throughout the day.
The sound quality is good and I was also quite surprised at the microphone quality which I tested out even though that's not really what I'm using it for. The mic was able to eliminate background sounds (e.g. a podcast playing in the background) while picking up me speaking normally.
These headphones also allow connecting simultaneously to 2 devices which is really convenient at work. Note this does not mean it can play sounds from both devices at the same time. Both are connected, and when one device becomes active, the headphones switch to that one automatically and pauses the other device. It does take a couple seconds for it to switch devices but I think that's expected. I have another headset that also allows 2 devices and operates similarly.
I was worried about sound leaking while wearing them in the office but at the volume I use them on, they are silent unless you're the wearer. This is also a volume that's suitable for hearing what's going on in the environment, which is what you would want open ear headphones for anyway.

*5.0 out of 5 stars*##### Love these! Super comfortable to wear, minimal sound leak
Reviewed in Canada on 12 July 2025
I've been looking for good open ear headphone especially for when I'm in the office since I want to be able to still hear what's going on around me. I have tried a couple cheaper alternatives with decent reviews, but found them very uncomfortable to wear on my ears, likely due to the shape of my ears. I'm very glad I decided to give this set a try because I found them EXTREMELY comfortable to wear, unlike others I've tried, and completely meets my needs! It barely feels like I'm wearing anything with these on and they don't press on the back of my ears at all. Note I do wear glasses most days and while my glasses make these a bit harder to put on securely, the headphones are still very comfortable to wear throughout the day.
The sound quality is good and I was also quite surprised at the microphone quality which I tested out even though that's not really what I'm using it for. The mic was able to eliminate background sounds (e.g. a podcast playing in the background) while picking up me speaking normally.
These headphones also allow connecting simultaneously to 2 devices which is really convenient at work. Note this does not mean it can play sounds from both devices at the same time. Both are connected, and when one device becomes active, the headphones switch to that one automatically and pauses the other device. It does take a couple seconds for it to switch devices but I think that's expected. I have another headset that also allows 2 devices and operates similarly.
I was worried about sound leaking while wearing them in the office but at the volume I use them on, they are silent unless you're the wearer. This is also a volume that's suitable for hearing what's going on in the environment, which is what you would want open ear headphones for anyway.

# Product Summary: OpenRock S2 Open Ear Headphones, Ultralight 7g, LDAC Hi-Res Audio, Triple Water Resistance, Bluetooth 6.0, Effortless Photography, Up to 32 Hours, Smart App, Clear Calls, Wireless Sports Headphones
From OpenRock
4.0 out of 5 stars, 150 ratings
[Customer reviews](?ref=dp_product_quick_view#customer-reviews_feature_div)
## Price
No featured offers available
[Other sellers](?ref=dp_product_quick_view#dynamic-aod-ingress-box)
[Other sellers](?ref=dp_product_quick_view#unqualifiedBuyBox)
## About this Item
* 7g Ultralight Hook-On Design For A Perfect Fit: Made with 0.6mm ultra-thin titanium filaments and soft liquid silicone, and weighing only 7g, OpenRock S2 flexibly adapts to different ear shapes, ensuring all-day comfort - even during outdoor activities.
* Enhanced Bass & Powerful Sound: OpenRock uses BassDirect technology to channel low-frequency energy from its 12mm transducer directly into the ear canal, delivering enhanced bass with minimal sound loss. With LDAC codec and Hi-Res certification, it supports high-resolution audio transmission, ensuring rich, detailed and high-quality sound.
* Triple Sweat & Water Resistant Design: Scientifically angled construction optimizes your wearing position, allowing sweat to glide away naturally and reducing contact with sweat. The independent BassDirect chamber protects PCBA components from sweat intrusion, while a water-repellent nano-coating on components improves durability.
* Effortless Photography with Remote Camera Control: Simply press the button on the headset to remotely control the camera when your phone is in photo or video mode, making capturing during outdoor hiking easy and convenient.
* 32 Hours Playtime: OpenRock S2 delivers up to 8 hours of playback on a single charge and up to 32 hours with the charging case. A 5-minute fast charge gives you 1 hour of use.
* AI Noise Cancellation with 4 Microphones: Four high-quality microphones use beamforming technology in array configuration, supporting an AI noise canceling algorithm to effectively eliminate ambient noise. With the windproof structure, even in strong winds, your call remains crystal clear.
* Bluetooth 6.0 & Multipoint Connection: OpenRock S2 is equipped with the latest Bluetooth 6.0 for fast transmission and instant pairing. Supports simultaneous connection to two Bluetooth devices with seamless switching.
## Product description
OpenRock S2 Open Ear Headphones, Wireless Bone Conduction Headphones
